### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-freiewähler.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Freie Wähler.

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 0 | 100% | 100% | Last Result, Median |
